SetDirectory joins any relative file paths with dir.\n// This method writes to config, and it's not concurrency safe.\nfunc (c *Config) SetDirectory(dir string) configurations including\n// the ones from the scrape_config_files.\n// This method does not write to config, and it's concurrency safe (the pointer receiver is for efficiency).\n// This method also assumes the Config was created by Load or LoadFile function, it returns error\n// if it was not. We can't re-validate or apply globals here due to races,\n// read more https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/15538.\nfunc (c *Config) GetScrapeConfigs() ([]*ScrapeConfig, error) {\n\tif !c.loaded {\n\t\t// Programmatic error, we warn before more confusing errors would happen due to lack of the globalization.\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"scrape config cannot be fetched, main config was not validated and loaded correctly; should not happen\")\n\t}\n\n\tscfgs := make([]*ScrapeConfig, len(c.ScrapeConfigs))\n\tjobNames := map[string]string{}\n\tfor i, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = \"main config file\"\n\t\tscfgs[i] = scfg\n\t}\n\n\t// Re-read and validate the dynamic scrape config rules.\n\tfor _, pat := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n\t\tfs, err := filepath.Glob(pat)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// The only error can be a bad pattern.\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error retrieving scrape config files for %q: %w\", pat, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, filename := range fs {\n\t\t\tcfg := ScrapeConfigs{}\n\t\t\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\terr = yaml.UnmarshalStrict(content, &cfg)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, scfg := range cfg.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\t\t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif f, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q, first found in %s\", scfg.JobName, f))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", filePath(filename))\n\n\t\t\t\tscfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filename))\n\t\t\t\tscfgs = append(scfgs, scfg)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn scfgs, nil\n}\n\n// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n// NOTE: This method should not be used outside of this package. Use Load or LoadFile instead.\nfunc (c *Config) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n\t*c = DefaultConfig\n\t// We want to set c to the defaults and then overwrite it with the input.\n\t// To make unmarshal fill the plain data struct rather than calling UnmarshalYAML\n\t// again, we have to hide it using a type indirection.\n\ttype plain Config\n\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// If a global block was open but empty the default global config is overwritten.\n\t// We have to restore it here.\n\tif c.GlobalConfig.isZero() {\n\t\tc.GlobalConfig = DefaultGlobalConfig\n\t}\n\n\t// If a runtime block was open but empty the default runtime config is overwritten.\n\t// We have to restore it here.\n\tif c.Runtime.isZero() {\n\t\tc.Runtime = DefaultRuntimeConfig\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, rf := range c.RuleFiles {\n\t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(rf) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid rule file path %q\", rf)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, sf := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n\t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(sf) {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid scrape config file path %q\", sf)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Do global overrides and validation.\n\tjobNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n\t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tif _, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q\", scfg.JobName)\n\t\t}\n\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tif err := c.AlertingConfig.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\trwNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, rwcfg := range c.RemoteWriteConfigs {\n\t\tif rwcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote write config section\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote write code.\n\t\tif _, ok := rwNames[rwcfg.Name]; ok && rwcfg.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote write configs with job name %q\", rwcfg.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif err := rwcfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\trwNames[rwcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\trrNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, rrcfg := range c.RemoteReadConfigs {\n\t\tif rrcfg == nil {\n\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote read config section\")\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote read code.\n\t\tif _, ok := rrNames[rrcfg.Name]; ok && rrcfg.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote read configs with job name %q\", rrcfg.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t\trrNames[rrcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GlobalConfig configures values that are used across other configuration\n// objects.\ntype GlobalConfig struct {\n\t// How frequently to scrape targets by default.\n\tScrapeInterval model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_interval,omitempty\"`\n\t// The default timeout when scraping targets.\n\tScrapeTimeout model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_timeout,omitempty\"`\n\t// The protocols to negotiate during a scrape. for scrape_timeout_seconds,\n\t// scrape_sample_limit, and scrape_body_size_bytes.\n\tExtraScrapeMetrics *bool `yaml:\"extra_scrape_metrics,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// ScrapeProtocol represents supported protocol for scraping metrics.\ntype ScrapeProtocol string\n\n// Validate returns error if given scrape protocol is not supported.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) Validate() error {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape protocol %v, supported: %v\",\n\t\t\ts, func() (ret []string) {\n\t\t\t\tfor k := range ScrapeProtocolsHeaders {\n\t\t\t\t\tret = append(ret, string(k))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ret)\n\t\t\t\treturn ret\n\t\t\t}())\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// HeaderMediaType returns the MIME mediaType for a particular ScrapeProtocol.\nfunc (s ScrapeProtocol) HeaderMediaType() string {\n\tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\tmediaType, _, err := mime.ParseMediaType(ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\treturn mediaType\n}\n\nvar (\n\tPrometheusProto      ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusProto\"\n\tPrometheusText0_0_4  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText0.0.4\"\n\tPrometheusText1_0_0  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText1.0.0\"\n\tOpenMetricsText0_0_1 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText0.0.1\"\n\tOpenMetricsText1_0_0 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText1.0.0\"\n\tUTF8NamesHeader      string         = model.EscapingKey + \"=\" + 281→\t}\n   282→\n   283→\tif attempt > 0 {\n   284→\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Retry-Attempt\", strconv.Itoa(attempt))\n   285→\t}\n   286→\n   287→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, c.timeout)\n   288→\tdefer cancel()\n   289→\n   290→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Store\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   291→\tdefer span.End()\n   292→\n   293→\thttpResp, err := c.Client.Do(httpReq.WithContext(ctx))\n   294→\tif err != nil {\n   295→\t\t// Errors from Client.Do are from (for example) network errors, so are\n   296→\t\t// recoverable.\n   297→\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, RecoverableError{err, defaultBackoff}\n   298→\t}\n   299→\tdefer func() {\n   300→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   301→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   302→\t}()\n   303→\n   304→\t// NOTE(bwplotka): Only PRW2 spec defines response HTTP headers. However, spec does not block\n   305→\t// PRW1 from sending them too for reliability. Support this case.\n   306→\t//\n   307→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   308→\t// Parsing error means there were some response header values we can't parse,\n   309→\t// we can continue handling.\n   310→\trs, _ := ParseWriteResponseStats(httpResp)\n   311→\n   312→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 2 {\n   313→\t\treturn rs, nil\n   314→\t}\n   315→\n   316→\t// Handling errors e.g. read potential error in the body.\n   317→\t// TODO(bwplotka): Pass logger and emit debug on error?\n   318→\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(io.LimitReader(httpResp.Body, maxErrMsgLen))\n   319→\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"server returned HTTP status %s: %s\", httpResp.Status, body)\n   320→\n   321→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 == 5 ||\n   322→\t\t(c.retryOnRateLimit && httpResp.StatusCode == http.StatusTooManyRequests) {\n   323→\t\treturn rs, RecoverableError{err, retryAfterDuration(httpResp.Header.Get(\"Retry-After\"))}\n   324→\t}\n   325→\treturn rs, err\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// retryAfterDuration returns the duration for the Retry-After header. In case of any errors, it\n   329→// returns the defaultBackoff as if the header was never supplied.\n   330→func retryAfterDuration(t string) model.Duration {\n   331→\tparsedDuration, err := time.Parse(http.TimeFormat, t)\n   332→\tif err == nil {\n   333→\t\ts := time.Until(parsedDuration).Seconds()\n   334→\t\treturn model.Duration(s) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   335→\t}\n   336→\t// The duration can be in seconds.\n   337→\td, err := strconv.Atoi(t)\n   338→\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\treturn defaultBackoff\n   340→\t}\n   341→\treturn model.Duration(d) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// Name uniquely identifies the client.\n   345→func (c *Client) Name() string {\n   346→\treturn c.remoteName\n   347→}\n   348→\n   349→// Endpoint is the remote read or write endpoint.\n   350→func (c *Client) Endpoint() string {\n   351→\treturn c.urlString\n   352→}\n   353→\n   354→// Read reads from a remote endpoint. The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   355→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   356→func (c *Client) Read(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   357→\treturn c.ReadMultiple(ctx, []*prompb.Query{query}, sortSeries)\n   358→}\n   359→\n   360→// ReadMultiple reads from a remote endpoint using multiple queries in a single request.\n   361→// The sortSeries parameter is only respected in the case of a samples response;\n   362→// chunked responses arrive already sorted by the server.\n   363→// Returns a single SeriesSet with interleaved series from all queries.\n   364→func (c *Client) ReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   365→\tc.readQueries.Inc()\n   366→\tdefer c.readQueries.Dec()\n   367→\n   368→\treq := &prompb.ReadRequest{\n   369→\t\tQueries:               queries,\n   370→\t\tAcceptedResponseTypes: c.acceptedResponseTypes,\n   371→\t}\n   372→\n   373→\thttpResp, cancel, start, err := c.executeReadRequest(ctx, req)\n   374→\tif err != nil {\n   375→\t\treturn nil, err\n   376→\t}\n   377→\n   378→\treturn c.handleReadResponse(httpResp, req, queries, sortSeries, start, cancel)\n   379→}\n   380→\n   381→// executeReadRequest creates and executes an HTTP request for reading data.\n   382→func (c *Client) executeReadRequest(ctx context.Context, req *prompb.ReadRequest) (*http.Response, context.CancelFunc, time.Time, error) {\n   383→\tdata, err := proto.Marshal(req)\n   384→\tif err != nil {\n   385→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to marshal read request: %w\", err)\n   386→\t}\n   387→\n   388→\tcompressed := snappy.Encode(nil, data)\n   389→\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(compressed))\n   390→\tif err != nil {\n   391→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to create request: %w\", err)\n   392→\t}\n   393→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   394→\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Accept-Encoding\", \"snappy\")\n   395→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/x-protobuf\")\n   396→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n   397→\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"X-Prometheus-Remote-Read-Version\", \"0.1.0\")\n   398→\n   399→\terrTimeout := fmt.Errorf(\"%w: request timed out after %s\", context.DeadlineExceeded, c.timeout)\n   400→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeoutCause(ctx, c.timeout, errTimeout)\n   401→\n   402→\tctx, span := otel.Tracer(\"\").Start(ctx, \"Remote Read\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))\n   403→\tdefer span.End()\n   404→\n   405→\tstart := time.Now()\n   406→\thttpResp, err := c.Client.Do(httpReq.WithContext(ctx))\n   407→\tif err != nil {\n   408→\t\tcancel()\n   409→\t\treturn nil, nil, time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"error sending request: %w\", err)\n   410→\t}\n   411→\n   412→\treturn httpResp, cancel, start, nil\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→// handleReadResponse processes the HTTP response and returns a SeriesSet.\n   416→func (c *Client) handleReadResponse(httpResp *http.Response, req *prompb.ReadRequest, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool, start time.Time, cancel context.CancelFunc) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   417→\tif httpResp.StatusCode/100 != 2 {\n   418→\t\t// Make an attempt at getting an error message.\n   419→\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   420→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   421→\n   422→\t\tcancel()\n   423→\t\terrStr := strings.Trim(string(body), \"\\n\")\n   424→\t\terr := errors.New(errStr)\n   425→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"remote server %s returned http status %s: %w\", c.urlString, httpResp.Status, err)\n   426→\t}\n   427→\n   428→\tcontentType := httpResp.Header.Get(\"Content-Type\")\n   429→\n   430→\tswitch {\n   431→\tcase strings.HasPrefix(contentType, \"application/x-protobuf\"):\n   432→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   433→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"sampled\", 438→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"chunked\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   439→\n   440→\t\ts := NewChunkedReader(httpResp.Body, c.chunkedReadLimit, nil)\n   441→\t\treturn 450→\t\tc.readQueriesDuration.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\").Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   451→\t\tc.readQueriesTotal.WithLabelValues(\"unsupported\", handleSampledResponse(req *prompb.ReadRequest, httpResp *http.Response, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   458→\tcompressed, err := io.ReadAll(httpResp.Body)\n   459→\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response. HTTP status code: %s: %w\", httpResp.Status, err)\n   461→\t}\n   462→\tdefer func() {\n   463→\t\t_, _ = io.Copy(io.Discard, httpResp.Body)\n   464→\t\t_ = httpResp.Body.Close()\n   465→\t}()\n   466→\n   467→\tuncompressed, err := snappy.Decode(nil, compressed)\n   468→\tif err != nil {\n   469→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading response: %w\", err)\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\tvar resp prompb.ReadResponse\n   473→\terr = proto.Unmarshal(uncompressed, &resp)\n   474→\tif err != nil {\n   475→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to unmarshal response body: %w\", err)\n   476→\t}\n   477→\n   478→\tif len(resp.Results) != len(req.Queries) {\n   479→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"responses: want %d, got %d\", len(req.Queries), len(resp.Results))\n   480→\t}\n   481→\n   482→\treturn combineQueryResults(resp.Results, sortSeries)\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→// combineQueryResults combines multiple query results into a single SeriesSet,\n   486→// handling both sorted and unsorted cases appropriately.\n   487→func combineQueryResults(results []*prompb.QueryResult, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error) {\n   488→\tif len(results) == 0 {\n   489→\t\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: nil, cur: 0}, nil\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\tif len(results) == 1 {\n   493→\t\treturn FromQueryResult(sortSeries, results[0]), nil\n   494→\t}\n   495→\n   496→\t// Multiple queries case - combine all results\n   497→\tif sortSeries {\n   498→\t\t// When sorting is requested, use MergeSeriesSet which can efficiently merge sorted inputs\n   499→\t\tvar allSeriesSets []storage.SeriesSet\n   500→\t\tfor _, result := range results {\n   501→\t\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   502→\t\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   503→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   504→\t\t\t}\n   505→\t\t\tallSeriesSets = append(allSeriesSets, seriesSet)\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t\treturn storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(allSeriesSets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge), nil\n   508→\t}\n   509→\n   510→\t// When sorting is not requested, just concatenate all series without using MergeSeriesSet\n   511→\t// since MergeSeriesSet requires sorted inputs\n   512→\tvar allSeries []storage.Series\n   513→\tfor _, result := range results {\n   514→\t\tseriesSet := FromQueryResult(sortSeries, result)\n   515→\t\tfor seriesSet.Next() {\n   516→\t\t\tallSeries = append(allSeries, seriesSet.At())\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\t\tif err := seriesSet.Err(); err != nil {\n   519→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error reading series from query result: %w\", err)\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t}\n   522→\n   523→\treturn &concreteSeriesSet{series: allSeries, cur: 0}, nil\n   524→}\n   525→\n   526→// handleChunkedResponseImpl handles chunked responses for both single and multiple queries.\n   527→func (*Client) handleChunkedResponseImpl(s *ChunkedReader, httpResp *http.Response, queries []*prompb.Query, onClose func(error)) storage.SeriesSet {\n   528→\t// For multiple queries in chunked response, we'll still use the existing infrastructure\n   529→\t// but we need to provide the timestamp range that covers all queries\n   530→\tvar minStartTs, maxEndTs int64 = math.MaxInt64, math.MinInt64\n   531→\n   532→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   533→\t\tminStartTs = min(minStartTs, query.StartTimestampMs)\n   534→\t\tmaxEndTs = max(maxEndTs, query.EndTimestampMs)\n   535→\t}\n   536→\n   537→\treturn NewChunkedSeriesSet(s, httpResp.Body, minStartTs, maxEndTs, onClose)\n   538→}\n   539→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. necessary.\ntype ReadClient interface {\n\tRead(ctx context.Context, query *prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n\tReadMultiple(ctx context.Context, queries []*prompb.Query, sortSeries bool) (storage.SeriesSet, error)\n}\n\n// NewReadClient creates a new client for remote read.\nfunc NewReadClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig, optFuncs ...config_util.HTTPClientOption) (ReadClient, error) {\n\thttpClient, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \"remote_storage_read_client\", optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tt := httpClient.Transport\n\tif len(conf.Headers) > 0 {\n\t\tt = newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(conf.Headers, t)\n\t}\n\thttpClient.Transport = otelhttp.NewTransport(t)\n\n\t// Set accepted response types, remoteReadQueryDuration.MustCurryWith(prometheus.Labels{remoteName: name, endpoint: conf.URL.String()}),\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// NewWriteClient creates a new client for remote write.\nfunc NewWriteClient(name string, conf *ClientConfig) (WriteClient, error) {\n\tvar httpOpts []config_util.HTTPClientOption\n\tif conf.RoundRobinDNS {\n\t\thttpOpts = newInjectHeadersRoundTripper(h map[string]string, underlyingRT http.RoundTripper) *injectHeadersRoundTripper {\n\treturn &injectHeadersRoundTripper{headers: h, RoundTripper: underlyingRT}\n}\n\ntype injectHeadersRoundTripper struct {\n\theaders map[string]string\n\thttp.RoundTripper\n}\n\nfunc (t *injectHeadersRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tfor key, value := range t.headers {\n\t\treq.Header.Set(key, value)\n\t}\n\treturn t.RoundTripper.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nconst defaultBackoff = 0\n\ntype RecoverableError struct {\n\terror\n\tretryAfter model.Duration\n}\n\n// Store sends a batch of samples to the HTTP endpoint, the request is the proto marshalled\n// and encoded bytes from codec.go.\nfunc (c *Client) Store(ctx context.Context, req []byte, attempt int) (WriteResponseStats, error) {\n\thttpReq, err := http.NewRequest(http.MethodPost, c.urlString, bytes.NewReader(req))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// Errors from NewRequest are from unparsable URLs, so are not\n\t\t// recoverable.\n\t\treturn WriteResponseStats{}, err\n\t}\n\n\thttpReq.Header.Add(\"Content-Encoding\", string(c.writeCompression))\n\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"Content-Type\", remoteWriteContentTypeHeaders[c.writeProtoMsg])\n\thttpReq.Header.Set(\"User-Agent\", UserAgent)\n\tif c.writeProtoMsg == remoteapi.WriteV1MessageType {\n\t\t// Compatibility mode for 1.0.\n\t\thttpReq.Header.Set(RemoteWriteVersionHeader, RemoteWriteVersion1HeaderValue)\n\t} else In case of any errors, it\n// returns the defaultBackoff as if the header was never supplied.\nfunc retryAfterDuration(t string) model.Duration {\n\tparsedDuration, err := time.Parse(http.TimeFormat, t)\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\ts := time.Until(parsedDuration).Seconds()\n\t\treturn model.Duration(s) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n\t}\n\t// The duration can be in seconds.\n\td, err := strconv.Atoi(t)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn defaultBackoff\n\t}\n\treturn model.Duration(d) * model.Duration(time.Second)\n}\n\n// Name uniquely identifies the client.\nfunc (c *Client) Name() string {\n\treturn c.remoteName\n}\n\n// Endpoint is the remote read or write endpoint.\nfunc (c *Client) Endpoint() string {\n\treturn c.urlString\n}\n\n// Read reads from a remote endpoint.
